! Title: AdBlock DNS Lite
! Description: 适用于 AdGuard、AdGuardHome 的去广告合并规则，每 8 个小时更新一次。规则源：AdGuard Base filter、AdGuard Chinese filter、AdGuard Mobile Ads filter、AdGuard DNS filter、uBlock filter、EasyList、EasyList China、EasyPrivacy、CJX's Annoyance List、xinggsf rule、xinggsf mv、SmartTV Blocklist、halflife、NoAppDownload、QuarkList、DD-AD、banad、Ad Filter J、Fuck Fuckadblock、GOODBYEADS、1Hosts (Lite)、AdRules DNS List、NEO DEV HOST、OISD Big、AWAvenue Ads Rule、d3ward、BlueSkyXN skyrules、mitv-blacklist、1024 hosts、ad-wars hosts、StevenBlack hosts、QuarkList hosts、ilpl、xiaobeita、WindowsSpyBlocker、eth-phishing-detect、Badd-Boyz-Hosts、URLhaus、DigitalSide Threat-Intel、dns-blocklists、newhosts-final、medium。Lite 版仅针对国内域名拦截。
